SUBENT        22412001   20110207                             22262241200100001 
BIB                 18         69                                 2241200100002 
TITLE      .Double-Differential Cross Sections from Inelastic     2241200100003 
            Neutron Scattering on Elemental Vanadium.             2241200100004 
COMMENT    .Elastic Scattering is not Included in Cross-Sections  2241200100005 
AUTHOR     (D.Schmidt,W.Mannhart,Zhou Chenwei)                    2241200100006 
INSTITUTE  (2GERPTB)     PTB, Braunschweig, Germany.              2241200100007 
REFERENCE  (C,97TRIEST,1,407,199705)  Proc. Int. Conf. NDST       2241200100008 
               Trieste, Italy (1997), Vol. 1, P.407-409           2241200100009 
EXP-YEAR   (1996)   Data Measured. 199711 - Data Published        2241200100010 
FACILITY   (CYCLO,2GERPTB) Turnable CV-28 compact cyclotron (1 ns 2241200100011 
                   pulse width) and multi-angle neutron           2241200100012 
                   Time-Of-Flight spectrometer.                   2241200100013 
DETECTOR   (SCIN)  Five NE213 neutron detectors located behind    2241200100014 
                   a massive collimator shielding in a distance   2241200100015 
             of 1200 cm from the sample. The angle separation     2241200100016 
             between the detectors is 12.5 deg.                   2241200100017 
             Detector's diameter 10.16 cm (D1)/ 25.40 cm (D2-D5), 2241200100018 
             length 2.54 cm (D1)/ 5.08 cm (D2-D5).                2241200100019 
             .The angle region covered is 12.5 deg to 160 deg.    2241200100020 
              An additional NE213 detector was used as relative   2241200100021 
              fluence monitor, diameter 3.81 cm, length 3.81 cm.  2241200100022 
              the movable monitor (in a fixed distance of 651 cm) 2241200100023 
              was always in a position of 58.9 deg relative       2241200100024 
              to the beam axis.                                   2241200100025 
METHOD     (TOF) Time-Of-Flight, 12 m flight path.                2241200100026 
           (PSD) n/gamma discrimination with pulse shape analysis.2241200100027 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA)  Polyethylene sample -          2241200100028 
               24.56 mm, height 49.74 mm, mass 22.46 g,           2241200100029 
               hydrogen content is 14.30 %.                       2241200100030 
INC-SOURCE (D-D) Deuterium gas target, 1.0 cm in diameter and     2241200100031 
                 3.0 cm in length, gas pressure 1.9 Hpa.          2241200100032 
                 Mean neutron energy is defined within +/- 20 keV.2241200100033 
SAMPLE     .Elemental vanadium, cylindrical sample, 99.8% purity, 2241200100034 
            diameter 25.0 mm, height 51.0 mm, mass 151.29 g,      2241200100035 
            placed 17.5 cm from the gas target centre.            2241200100036 
CORRECTION .Monte-Carlo simulated TOF spectra of the complete     2241200100037 
            angular distribution were iteratively adjusted to     2241200100038 
            the measured TOF spectra. The simulation comprised    2241200100039 
            the neutron production in the gas target and the      2241200100040 
            scattering geometry between target, sample and        2241200100041 
            detectors.                                            2241200100042 
            .Parasitic neutrons from the D(d,np) breakup reaction 2241200100043 
            were simulated and subtracted. The data for the       2241200100044 
            simulation were adjusted by additional measurements   2241200100045 
            Of the neutron scattering with a 4He(d,np) neutron    2241200100046 
            source (only breakup neutrons).                       2241200100047 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T)  Total errors comprise counting statistics and 2241200100048 
                    systematic contributions of                   2241200100049 
           (ERR-1)  - Error of Detectors' Efficiency (2%),        2241200100050 
           (ERR-2)  - Angle Uncertainty (0.2 DEG),                2241200100051 
           (ERR-3)  - Multiple Scattering Correction (5%).        2241200100052 
           (ERR-4)  - An Additional Uncertainty of 5% of the      2241200100053 
             Ratio N-Bu/N-In is Taken Into Account (N-BU =        2241200100054 
             subtracted fraction of scattered breakup neutrons,   2241200100055 
             N-IN = fraction of inelastically scattered neutrons  2241200100056 
             after breakup subtraction).                          2241200100057 
           (MONIT-ERR)     - N-P scattering error(1%),            2241200100058 
ANALYSIS    The double-differential inelastic cross sections were 2241200100059 
            extracted as elemental cross sections.                2241200100060 
COVARIANCE .           Complete covariance matrices of the fitted 2241200100061 
                Legendre coefficients are available upon request  2241200100062 
                from the authors                                  2241200100063 
                ( E-MAIL: DANKWART.SCHMIDT@PTB.DE ).              2241200100064
